  161. I am not a huge hairspray user. I have curly hair, but, I tend to prefer gel and other hold products to style my hair because of the risk of crispy hair or sticky residue. This hairspray has done a fairly decent job on it's own, but, I am not 100% in love with this product. The first time that I used it, I used the product as indicated on the packaging (with a little help from other users of the product). I washed and styled my hair as usual (co-wash, leave-in condish, curl keeper, hard hold hair gel) and let it dry most of the way. Then, I worked in sections and spritzed Sprunch into my hair and scrunched it. I didn't really notice any additional hold and I didn't really notice any sort of curl enhancing benefits to using it in this manner. However, I used it on fourth-day hair later in the week and it did much better things for my hair. I styled my hair that day by first spritzing my hair with some plain water and then flipping my head upside down and spritzing the bottom layer with Sprunch. I scrunched those sections of my hair and then flipped upright. I already noticed a huge difference when I righted myself. The bottom layer had a bit more wave in it than it usually does on the fourth-day (it's all usually pretty straight at that point). I worked through the rest of my hair, lifting sections and spritzing Sprunch on them, first focusing on the lengths and then hitting the roots a bit. I did my whole head and my hair turned out pretty awesome for fourth-day hair! I usually have to topknot on the third-day and wash and style my hair, so, getting my hair to go into a fourth day was pretty excellent. The only reason I gave this product four stars instead of five is that it won't be an every day product for me because it certainly isn't a routine changer. But, it's a great product to use to refresh my hair if I'm not quite ready to wash it yet. Another reason for only giving it four stars is that I won't be using this product too regularly. While the silicone in the product is OK to use for modified curly girl routines and can be removed with a gentle low-poo, I don't always low-poo, and certainly try to avoid it as much as I possibly can in the cooler/dry months of the year. All in all, this is a pretty decent product and other people might enjoy it as much, if not more, than I have enjoyed using Sprunch. It does give you extra volume and wavy definition, so, this might be a great product to use in the summer if you want beachy waves/curls.
